hrīṃ iti mṛdbījam | prakāśam- oṃ hrīṃ bhagavati bagalāmukhi devi   
sarvaduṣṭānāṃ vācaṃ mukhaṃ padaṃ stambhaya 2 jihvāṃ kīlaya 2 buddhiṃ   
vināśaya 2 hrīṃ oṃ svāhā (52) iti || athendrākṣyā mantroddhāraḥ   
rudrayāmale-  
  
tryakṣaṃ kuntīdvayaṃ devi kūrcayugmaṃ tathaiva ca |  
prasthabījaṃ parāṃ padmāṃ carmāṇaṃ ca tato'bhidhām || 1 ||  
  
indrākṣi vajrahaste'nte lakṣmīṃ lajjāṃ ca puṣkaram |  
tīrayugmaṃ rasane dve trāsaścandro haraṃ vanam || 2 ||  
  
indrākṣyā devadevyāśca hyaṣṭāviṃśākṣaro manuḥ |  
  
tatra prasthabījanāmāni śāradāpaṭale-   
  
prasthabījaṃ sānubījaṃ śikharaṃ puṣkaraṃ tathā |  
mlauṃ bījoddhārametaddhi cānyadanṛtamāvadet || 1 ||  
  
prakāśam- oṃ krīṃ krīṃ hūṃ hūṃ mlauṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ aiṃ indrākṣi   
vajrahaste śrīṃ hrīṃ mlauṃ hūṃ hūṃ krīṃ krīṃ oṃ aiṃ phaṭ svāhā   
(28) iti ||  
  
śrī-īśvaraḥ |  
  
tisra etā mayā khyātā devi bhuvanadevatāḥ |  
dakṣiṇāmūrtinā bhaktyā saṃsāre'smin prakāśitāḥ || 1 ||  
  
athāhaṃ devadeveśi khecaryā vacmi vai manum |  
yāmāśritya labhedyogī khecarīṃ siddhidāṃ kalām || 2 ||  
  
viśvayāmale khecarīmantroddhāraḥ-  
  
gīrbāṇadaśamaṃ varṇaṃ coddharet pratilomataḥ |  
tamobījaṃ tato dadyānmāyābījaṃ tataḥ param || 1 ||  
  
tato dadyāccharadbījaṃ kūṭo'yaṃ parikīrtitaḥ |  
  
p. 562)  
  
mantraṃ (bījaṃ) turyaśiro jñeyaṃ yogī dadyāttato'bhidhām || 2 ||  
  
khecaryai ca tato dadyādante hyauśmakameva ca |  
  
prakāśam- mūlhrīṃsauḥ phecaryai namaḥ iti ||  
  
iti śrīdakṣiṇāmūrtimuniviracite uddhārakośe sarvāgamasāre tridevīnāṃ   
khecaryāśca kośākhyānaṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ kalpaḥ || 6 ||  
atha  
  
saptamaḥ kalpaḥ |  
  
śrī-īśvaraḥ |  
  
atha vakṣyāmi te devi dhyānānāgamaniścitān |  
etāsāṃ devatānāṃ tvaṃ śṛṇu pārvati tattvataḥ || 1 ||  
  
tatrādau daśavidyānāṃ dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi tvaṃ śṛṇu |  
vāmakeśvara tantroktaṃ tripurāyāḥ sureśvari || 2 ||  
  
divyāmbarāṅkitatanuṃ mihirāgnicandranetrāṃ sudhāṃśumukuṭāṃ   
himasannibhābhām |  
siṃhāsanāṃ paraśukhaḍgadharāṃ bhujābhyāṃ brahmendraviṣṇunamitāṃ   
tripurāṃ bhaje'ham || 3 ||  
  
atha vakṣye śriyo dhyānaṃ bhāṣitaṃ rudrayāmale |  
munisādhakagīrvāṇa vighnavargaiḥ [kh: vipravargaiḥ] supūjitam || 4 ||  
  
lakṣmīṃ padmāsanagatakaṭiṃ sūryaśītāṃśunetrāmudyadbhāsvatkanakarucibhiḥ   
padmaśaṅkhāsipāṇim |  
  
p. 563)  
  
nānāmuktāmaṇisukalaśāṃ bhūṣitāṅgīṃ dvibāhuṃ nityaṃ lokatritayaphaladāṃ   
naumyahaṃ bhaktipūrvam || 5 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi vāgdevyā dhyānaṃ vidyāpradaṃ śive |  
tantramuktāvalau granthe durlabhe tridive'pi ca || 6 ||  
  
vāṇīṃ pūrṇaniśākarojjvalamukhīṃ karpūrakundaprabhāṃ   
candrārdhāṅkitamastakāṃ nijakaraiḥ saṃbibhratīmādarāt |  
vīṇāmakṣaguṇaṃ sudhāḍhyakalaśaṃ vidyāṃ ca tuṅgastanīṃ   
divyairābharaṇairvibhūṣitatanuṃ siṃhādhirūḍhāṃ bhaje || 7 ||  
  
adha vakṣyāmi tārāyā dhyānaṃ bhairavatantrake |  
devyā bhedavihīnāyā munisādhakapūjite || 8 ||  
  
devīṃ pannagabhūṣitāṃ himaruciṃ śītāṃśuśaṅkhaprabhāṃ   
muktāratnaparītakaṇṭhavalayāṃ raktāmbaraṃ bibhratīm |  
śūlābjāsigadādharāṃ suragaṇairvaikuṇṭhamukhyaiḥ stutāṃ nityaṃ   
lokatrayaikarakṣaṇaparāṃ tārāṃ trinetrāṃ bhaje || 9 ||  
  
athāhaṃ bhuvaneśvaryā dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi tacchṛṇu |  
sādhakeṣṭaprade granthe niḥsṛtaṃ rudrayāmale || 10 ||  
  
udyadbhānusahasrasannibhamukhīṃ pīnastanīṃ padmagāṃ   
dorbhiraṅkuśapāśapustakajapān [kh: jayān] saṃbibhratīṃ sādaram |  
brahmopendramaheśvarendramunibhirnityaṃ stutāṃ vandanaiḥ   
stotrādyairbhuvaneśvarīṃ trinayanāṃ hṛtpaṅkaje'haṃ bhaje || 11 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi mātaṅgyā dhyānaṃ parvatanandini |  
kubjikāsarvasve granthe mamāpyatyantadurlabhe || 12 ||  
  
candrārdhāṅkitaśekharāṃ trinayanāṃ koṭīndusūryaprabhāṃ  
nānāratnasahasrabaddharaśanāṃ pretāsane saṃsthitām |  
  
p. 564)  
  
śaṅkhaṃ tomarapaṭṭisābjayugalān dorbhirvahantīṃ mudā dhyāye'haṃ hṛdaye   
sadā bhagavatīṃ mātaṅginīṃ hāriṇīm || 13 ||  
  
atha vakṣye maheśāni śārikādhyānamuttamam |  
āgamāmṛtamañjaryāṃ niḥsṛtaṃ durlabhaṃ janaiḥ || 14 ||  
  
śrīśaṅkhacakramusalāmbujayugmahastāṃ [g: salābjayugāṅka]  
nāgendrahāravalayāṅkitakaṇṭhamālām |  
sindūrakuṅkumasahasramarīcidīptiṃ śrīśārikāṃ trinayanāṃ hṛdaye smarāmi ||   
15 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi deveśi rājñīdhyānamanuttamam |  
vāmakeśvaratantroktaṃ parvateśvaranandini || 16 ||  
  
śītāṃśubālārkakṛśānunetrāṃ caturbhujāmeṇatvagāsanasthām |  
śaṅkhābjaśūlāsidharāṃ maheśīṃ rājñīṃ bhaje'haṃ tuhinādrirūpām || 17 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi bhīḍāyā dhyānamicchāphalapradam |  
niḥsṛtamāgamoddyote mayā viracite svayam || 18 ||  
  
udyacchītāṃśuraśmidyuticayasadṛśīṃ phullapadmopaviṣṭāṃ   
vīṇānāgendraśaṅkhāyudhaparaśudharāṃ dorbhirīḍyaiścaturbhiḥ |  
muktāhārāṃśunānāmaṇiyutahṛdayāṃ śīdhupātraṃ vahantīṃ vande bhīḍāṃ   
bhavānīṃ prahasitavadanāṃ sādhakeṣṭapradātrīm || 19 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi deveśi jvālāmukhyā anuttamam |  
dhyānaṃ mayā viracite granthe jvālāśiromaṇau || 20 ||  
  
jvālāparītāsyaśiroruhāṃ tāṃ sarojaśaṅkhāsigadādharāṃ ca |  
  
p. 565)  
  
siṃhāsanasthāpitapādayugmāṃ jvālāmukhīṃ saddhṛdaye smarāmi || 21 ||  
  
athāhaṃ bhadrakālyāśca dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi niḥsṛtam |  
svayaṃ mayā viracite tantre vai vāmakeśvare || 22 ||  
  
muṇḍaṃ viśvasya kartuḥ karakamalatale dhārayantīṃ hasantīṃ nāhaṃ tṛptā   
vadantīṃ sakalajanamidaṃ bhakṣayantīṃ sadaiva |  
śyāmāṃ viṣṇuṃ girīśaṃ bhujanivahabalācchūlaprotaṃ vahantīṃ dhyāye'haṃ   
bhadrakālīṃ navajaladanibhāṃ pretamadhyāsanasthām || 23 ||  
  
turīdhyānamahaṃ vakṣye niḥsṛtamāgamāmṛte |  
asmiṃścarācare khyāte brahmaṇaiva prakāśite || 24 ||  
  
nānāratnanibaddhacandraśakalāṃ maulau jaṭābhirvṛte pāśāmbhojadharāṃ   
himāṃśudhavalāṃ dorbhyāṃ dvibāhuṃ śivām |  
sūryendvagnivilocanāṃ smitamukhīṃ pretāsane saṃsthitāṃ   
brahmopendramaheśvaraiśca namitāṃ devīṃ bhaje'haṃ turīm || 25 ||  
  
athāhaṃ [g: athādau] chinnamastāyā dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi niḥsṛtam |  
svakṛte tripurāyāśca granthe devi śiromaṇau || 26 ||  
  
eṇāṅkāṃśuparītabhālaphalakāṃ bālārkakoṭiprabhāṃ   
jvālābaddhamahārgharatnanicayāṃ kandarpadarpojjvalām |  
śūlāsyaṅkuśapāśaveṇumusalāmbhojābhayān bibhratīṃ bhakteṣṭāṃ [g:   
bhaktaiḥ pūjitapādapadmayugalāṃ śrīcchinnamastāṃ bhaje]   
chinnamastakāṃ bhagavatīṃ dhyāye hṛdabje sadā || 27 ||  
  
dakṣiṇākālikāyāśca dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi niḥsṛtam |  
granthe kālīrahasye'smin parvateśvaranandini || 28 ||  
  
brahmopendraśivāsthimuṇḍaraśanāṃ tāmbūlaraktādharāṃ varṣāmeghanibhāṃ   
triśūlamusale padmāsipāśāṅkuśān |  
  
p. 566)  
  
śaṅkhaṃ sāhiyugaṃ varaṃ daśabhujaiḥ saṃvibhratīṃ pretagāṃ devīṃ   
dakṣiṇakālikāṃ bhagavatīṃ raktāmbarāṃ tāṃ smare || 29 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi śyāmāyā dhyānaṃ parvatanandini |  
śyāmātantre mayākhyātaṃ sakalāgamasāgare || 30 ||  
  
trailokyapūjitapadāmburuhadvayāṃ tāṃ kṛṣṇāmbubhṛtsadṛśarūpadharāṃ   
trinetrām |  
śūlāsiśaṅkhamahatīśca bhujairvahantīṃ śyāmāṃ bhaje   
śavaśarīrakṛtāsanasthām || 31 ||  
  
athāhaṃ kālarātryāste dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi niḥsṛtam |  
mayā viracite devi tantre vai vāmakeśvare || 32 ||  
  
śūlābjapāśāṅkuśapadmahastāṃ caturbhujāṃ dhūmranibhāṃ trinetrām |  
siṃhāsanasthāṃ dhṛtapītavastrāṃ dhyāye maheśīṃ hṛdi kālarātrīm || 33 ||  
  
nānābharaṇasaṃyukte devi vakṣyāmi tvaṃ śṛṇu |  
śrīvajrayoginīdhyānaṃ niḥsṛtaṃ kulikārṇave || 34 ||  
  
indvagnisūryanayanāṃ pāśāṅkuśadharāṃ śivām [k: parāṃ; g:   
śubhāṃ] |  
dvibhujāṃ siṃhamadhyasthāṃ bhaje'haṃ vajrayoginīm [k, g, gh:   
abhayaṅkarīm] || 35 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi vārāhyā dhyānaṃ tantraviniścitam |  
yathābhīṣṭapradaṃ devi kulacūḍāmaṇau priye || 36 ||  
  
candrārdhacūḍāṃ dvibhujāṃ bhujābhyāṃ śūlāṅkuśau śyāmamukhīṃ   
vahantīm |  
sūryāgnicandrīkṛtanetrapadmāṃ [k: dṛṣṭipātāṃ] dhyāye hṛdabje   
vimalāṃ varāhīm || 37 ||  
  
p. 567)  
  
atha vakṣyāmi deveśi śāradādhyānamuttamam |  
śāradāpaṭale granthe racite'pi mayā svayam || 38 ||  
  
ṣaḍbhujāṃ trinayanāṃ smitānanāṃ śāṇḍilyarṣinutapādapaṅkajām |  
parvatasthitavatīṃ dhṛtaśūlāṃ śāradāṃ bhagavatīṃ hṛdi dhyāye || 39 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi deveśi tvaṃ śṛṇu dhyānamuttamam |  
kāmeśvaryāstripurāyāḥ sarvasve tantrakottame || 40 ||  
  
trilocanāṃ sūryasahasraśobhāṃ siṃhāsanasthāṃ dvibhujāṃ dhṛtāsim |  
pītāmbarāṃ viṣṇumaheśasevyāṃ kāmeśvarīṃ tāṃ hṛdaye smarāmi || 41 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi gauryāste dhyānaṃ bhairavatantrake |  
granthe mayā viracite parvateśvaranandini || 42 ||  
  
gaurāṅgīṃ dhṛtapaṅkajāṃ trinayanāṃ śvetāmbarāṃ siṃhagāṃ   
candrodbhāsitaśekharāṃ smitamukhīṃ dorbhyāṃ vahantīṃ gadām |  
viṣṇvindrāmbujayoniśambhutridaśaiḥ saṃpūjitāṅghridvayāṃ gaurīṃ   
mānasapaṅkaje bhagavatīṃ bhakteṣṭadāṃ tāṃ bhaje || 43 ||  
  
athāhamannapūrṇāyā dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi tvaṃ śṛṇu |  
niḥsṛtaṃ bhairavītantre mayā devi prakāśite || 44 ||  
  
candrārdhamauliṃ dvibhujāṃ trinetrāṃ śūlākṣamāle dvibhuje vahantīm |  
eṇāsanasthāṃ bhujagopavītāṃ tāmannapūrṇāṃ hṛdaye smarāmi || 45 ||  
  
kulavāgīśvarīdhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi tvaṃ śṛṇu priye |  
  
p. 568)  
  
āgamāmṛtamañjaryāṃ durlabhāyāṃ mamāpi ca || 46 ||  
  
triśūlāsidharāṃ dorbhyāṃ raktāsyāṃ vahnisannibhām |  
tryakṣāṃ siṃhāsanagatāṃ kulavāgīśvarīṃ bhaje || 47 ||  
  
atha vakṣye gaṇeśasya dhyānaṃ gīrbāṇapūjite |  
āgamāmṛtapīyūṣe [ g: rṇava] durlabhe bhuvane'mbike || 48 ||  
  
dvicaturdaśavarṇabhūṣitāṅgaṃ musalāmbhojadharoragopavītam |  
dvimṛgādhipagāminaṃ trinetraṃ śivaputraṃ dviradānanaṃ bhaje'ham || 49 ||  
  
atha dhyānaṃ kumārasya vakṣyāmi śṛṇu pārvati |  
niḥsṛtamāgamoddyote mayā viracite svayam || 50 ||  
  
himādrigauraṃ [g: śvetaṃ] dvibhujaṃ bhujaṅgaiḥ parītagātraṃ   
śikhiviṣṭarastham |  
nagendrakanyāpriyaputramādyaṃ hṛdi smare'bhīṣṭapradaṃ kumāram || 51 ||  
  
haihayasya bravīmyevaṃ dhyānaṃ tava kutūhalāt |  
yathābhīṣṭapradaṃ nṝṇāmuḍḍāmaraviniścitam || 52 ||  
  
sahasrabhujamaṇḍalījitatamīcareśādhipaṃ himāṃśusadṛśānanaṃ   
dhṛtasahasratūṇīrakam |  
sitāmbaradharaṃ sadā turagarājamadhyasthitaṃ smarāmi bhuvanādhipaṃ hṛdi tu   
kārtavīryārjunam || 23 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi deveśi dhyānaṃ tasya viniḥsṛtam |  
mṛtyuñjayasya devasya granthe kubjāśiromaṇau || 54 ||  
  
p. 569)  
  
candrodbhāsitamūrdhajaṃ surapatiṃ pīyūṣapātraṃ bṛhad hastābjena   
sudhāṃśukoṭivimalaṃ hastasthapaṅkeruham [g: candrāmṛtāplāvitaṃ]   
|  
sūryāgnīnduvilocanaṃ karatalaiḥ   
pāśākṣasūtrāṅkuśāmbhojānvibhratamakṣayaṃ paśupatiṃ mṛtyuñjayaṃ   
taṃ smare || 55 ||  
  
sugrīvasyātha vakṣye'haṃ dhyānaṃ parvatanandini |  
kulacūḍāmaṇau granthe nirmite mantrasāgare || 56 ||  
  
bālaṃ ṣoḍaśahāyanaṃ kapipatiṃ vahniprabhābhāsvaraṃ   
dorbhirvṛkṣagadādhanuḥśaracayān saṃbibhrataṃ cādarāt [g: sādarāt]  
sītāmārgaṇasaktavānarabalairārādhyamānaṃ bhaje kākutsthaṃ   
bhajamānamarkatanayaṃ sugrīvadevaṃ hṛdi || 57 ||  
  
athāhaṃ te hanumato dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi niḥsṛtam |  
kulacūḍāmaṇau granthe parvateśvaranandini || 58 ||  
  
rāmeṣṭamitraṃ jagadekavīraṃ plavaṅgarājendrakṛtapraṇāmam |  
sumeruśṛṅgābhamacintyamādyaṃ hṛdi smare'haṃ hanumantamīḍyam || 59 ||  
  
atha te bhairavasyāhaṃ dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi pārvati |  
niḥsṛtaṃ bhairave tantre yathābhīṣṭaphalapradam || 60 ||  
  
kapālahastaṃ bhujagopavītaṃ kṛṣṇacchaviṃ daṇḍadharaṃ trinetram |  
acintyamādyaṃ madhupānasaktaṃ hṛdi smare bhairavamiṣṭadaṃ tam || 61 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi sūryasya dhyānaṃ tantraviniścitam |  
  
p. 570)  
  
tripurāsarvasve granthe dakṣiṇāmūrtinā kṛte || 62 ||  
  
pratyakṣadevaṃ viśadaṃ sahasramarīcibhiḥ śobhitabhūmideśam |  
saptāśvagaṃ saddhvajahastamādyaṃ devaṃ bhaje'haṃ mihiraṃ hṛdabje || 63 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi saumyasya dhyānaṃ bhairavatantrake |  
yathābhīṣṭapradaṃ satyaṃ surāsuranamaskṛte || 64 ||  
  
somātmajaṃ haṃsagataṃ dvibāhuṃ śaṅkhendurūpaṃ hyasipāśahastam |  
dayānidhiṃ bhūṣaṇabhūṣitāṅgaṃ budhaṃ smare mānasapaṅkaje'ham || 65 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi śukrasya dhyānaṃ tantraviniścitam |  
kubjikāsarvasve granthe brahmaṇaiva prakāśite || 66 ||  
  
santaptakāñcananibhaṃ dvibhujaṃ dayāluṃ pītāmbaraṃ   
dhṛtasaroruhadvandvaśūlam |  
krauñcāsanaṃ hyasurasevitapādapadmaṃ śukraṃ smare dvinayanaṃ hṛdi   
paṅkaje'ham || 67 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi jīvasya śṛṇu pārvati tattvataḥ |  
dhyānaṃ bhairavatantroktaṃ sakalārthapradaṃ nṛṇām || 68 ||  
  
tejomayaṃ śaktitriśūlahastaṃ surendrajyeṣṭhaiḥ stutapādapadmam |  
medhānidhiṃ hastigataṃ [g: matsya] dvibāhuṃ guruṃ smare   
mānasapaṅkaje'ham || 69 ||  
  
p. 571)  
  
atha vakṣyāmi candrasya dhyānaṃ devi śṛṇu priye |  
niḥsṛtamāgamoddyote nānādhyānasaritpatau || 70 ||  
  
śaṅkhaprabhameṇapriyaṃ śaśāṅkamīśānamaulisthitamīḍyavṛttam [g:   
rūpam] |  
tamīpatiṃ nīrajayugmahastaṃ [k: mambuja] dhyāye hṛdabje śaśinaṃ   
graheśam || 71 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi bhaumasya dhyānaṃ tantraviniścitam |  
āgamāmṛtamañjaryāṃ śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ priye || 72 ||  
  
prataptagāṅgeyanibhaṃ graheśaṃ siṃhāsanasthaṃ kamalāsihastam |  
surāsuraiḥ pūjitapādapadmaṃ bhaumaṃ dayāluṃ hṛdaye smarāmi || 73 ||  
  
atha vakṣye śanerdhyānaṃ yathābhīṣṭaphalapradam |  
niḥsṛtaṃ ca maheśāni śubhadamāgamāmṛte || 74 ||  
  
nīlāñjanābhaṃ mihireṣṭaputraṃ graheśvaraṃ pāśabhujaṅgapāṇim |  
surāsurāṇāṃ bhayadaṃ dvibāhuṃ śaniṃ smare mānasapaṅkaje'ham || 75 ||  
  
athāhaṃ saiṃhikeyasya dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi tvaṃ śṛṇu |  
niḥsṛtaṃ phaladaṃ nṝṇāṃ tantre vai vāmakeśvare || 76 ||  
  
śītāṃśumitrāntakamīḍyarūpaṃ ghoraṃ ca vaiḍūryanibhaṃ vibāhum |  
trailokyarakṣāparamiṣṭadaṃ [g: pradaṃ] ca rāhuṃ grahendraṃ hṛdaye   
smarāmi || 77 ||  
  
p. 572)  
  
atha vakṣyāmi ketośca dhyānamāgamaniścitam |  
niḥsṛtamāgamoddyote granthe vai tantrasāgare [kh: mantra] || 78 ||  
  
lāṅgulayuktaṃ bhayadaṃ janānāṃ kṛṣṇāmbubhṛtsannibhamekavīram |  
kṛṣṇāmbaraṃ śaktitriśūlahastaṃ ketuṃ bhaje mānasapaṅkaje'ham || 79 ||  
  
atha vakṣyāmi deveśi bhavānīdhyānamuttamam |  
kulacūḍāmaṇau granthe niḥsṛtaṃ bhuvaneśvari || 80 ||  
  
ariśaṅkhakṛpāṇakheṭabāṇān sudhanuḥśūlakatarjanīrdadhānām [k:   
rdadhānā | bhavatāṃ mahiṣottamāṅgasaṃsthā navadūrvāsadṛśī śriye'stu   
durgā] |  
bhayadāṃ mahiṣottamāṅgasaṃsthāṃ navadūrvāsadṛśīṃ bhaje bhavānīm || 81   
||  
  
athāhaṃ bagalāmukhyā dhyānaṃ vakṣyāmi niḥsṛtam |  
āgamāmṛtamañjaryāṃ surāsuranamaskṛte || 82 ||  
  
nānāratnanibaddharamyamukuṭāṃ pītāmbarāṃ bhāgyadāṃ  
gharmāṃśvagniśaśāṅkaraśminayanāṃ siṃhāsanasthāṃ śivām |  
saccaṇḍīśaratāṃ [k: saccaṇḍāṃśunibhāṃ; g: sadragāṅgeyanibhāṃ]   
mahārghamaṇibhirudbhāsitāṅgīṃ sadā devīṃ śrībagalāmukhīṃ hṛdi bhaje   
bhakteṣṭadāṃ muktidām || 83 ||  
  
atha vakṣye śṛṇoṣi tvamindrākṣīdhyānamuttamam |  
niḥsṛtaṃ jagadīśāni granthe vai rudrayāmale || 84 ||  
  
p. 573)  
  
mālāsyaṅkuśapadmayugmakadharāṃ cakṣuḥsahasrāṅkitāṃ [g:   
sāhasranetrāṃ śivāṃ] mattairāvaṇapṛṣṭhagāṃ śaśimukhīṃ   
trailokyarakṣāparām |  
dorbhirgānaratāṃ sphuṭāmbujanibhāṃ brahmādidevaiḥ stutāmindrākṣīṃ   
janamātaraṃ hṛdi bhaje kāruṇyarūpāṃ parām || 85||  
  
atha vakṣye maheśāni khecarīdhyānamuttamam |  
  
yāṃ dhyātvā khecarīṃ yogī jīvanmukto bhavet kalau |  
granthe bhairavatantrākhye niḥsṛtaṃ tridaśārcite || 86 ||  
  
vinindrakamalotpalairmunibhirarcitāṅghridvayāṃ sitāṃ sitakarāmbujāṃ   
sitakarojjvalacchekharām |  
ravīnduśikhilocanāmabhayapustakau bibhratīṃ smarāmi hṛdi khecarīṃ   
bhuvanamātaraṃ siddhidām || 87 ||  
  
etāsāṃ devadeveśi mantradhyānacayaṃ smṛtam |  
yasya kasya na dātavyaṃ granthamuddhārakośakam || 88 ||  
  
ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ |  
  
dhanyaḥ sa yasya putrastvaṃ sakalāgamapāragaḥ |  
jaya tvaṃ svagṛhaṃ gantumājñāpayitumarhasi || 89 ||  
  
dakṣiṇāmūrtiḥ |  
  
gacchadhvaṃ munayaḥ sarve kṣamadhvaṃ kṛpayā mama |  
ityuktvā munayo jagmuḥ svagṛhaṃ mantralālasāḥ || 90 ||  
  
śrī-īśvara uvāca |  
  
dakṣiṇāmūrtinā tena dṛṣṭvā tantrānmanoramān |  
kṛtamuddhārakośākhyaṃ granthaṃ gopyatamaṃ kuru || 91 ||  
  
p. 574)  
  
śrīdevyuvāca |  
  
krītāsmi bhavatānena granthenāhaṃ sureśvara |  
ityuktvā sumahākuñjaṃ kailāsādreśca jagmatuḥ |  
ubhau tāvambikā devī devaśca candraśekharaḥ || 92 ||  
  
iti śrīdakṣiṇāmūrtimuniviracite uddhārakośe sarvāgamasāre ṣoḍaśadevī   
saptadevī saptakumāra navagraha tridevī khecarīdhyānakośanirūpaṇaṃ saptamaḥ   
kalpaḥ || 7 ||  
  
samāptaścāyamuddhārakośa iti śivam |
